High Court Rules Muratina Not Illicit Brew

06 Jul 2024, 00:00

The High Court sitting in Kiambu has declared that Muratina, a traditional drink of the Agikuyu community, is not an illicit brew. The ruling came as part of a Constitutional petition centered on preserving traditional practices and culture. Judge Mushila, presiding over the case involving 12 petitioners, stated that Muratina does not fall under the category of illicit brews. This decision affirms the Agikuyu people’s right to prepare and consume Muratina as an integral part of their cultural and traditional heritage.
